    SELECT [p4].[ProductoMaterialID], [p4].[MaterialID], [p4].[Porcentaje], [p4].[ProductoID], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [m0].[Estado], [m0].[Nombre]

    INNER JOIN [Materiales] AS [m0] ON [p4].[MaterialID] = [m0].[MaterialID]
) AS [t3] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [t3].[ProductoID]

INNER JOIN [CategoriasPrincipales] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoriaPrincipalID] = [c].[CategoriaPrincipalID]
INNER JOIN [Marcas] AS [m] ON [p].[MarcaID] = [m].[MarcaID]
INNER JOIN [TiposProducto] AS [t] ON [p].[TipoProductoID] = [t].[TipoProductoID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductoImagenes] AS [p0] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [p0].[ProductoID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductoStockVariantes] AS [p1] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [p1].[ProductoID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p2].[ProductoTallaID], [p2].[ProductoID], [p2].[StockTalla], [p2].[TallaID], [t1].[TallaID] AS [TallaID0], [t1].[Nombre], [t1].[Orden]
    FROM [ProductoTallas] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tallas] AS [t1] ON [p2].[TallaID] = [t1].[TallaID]
) AS [t0] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [t0].[ProductoID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p3].[ProductoColorID], [p3].[ColorID], [p3].[ProductoID], [c0].[ColorID] AS [ColorID0], [c0].[CodigoHex], [c0].[Estado], [c0].[Nombre]
    FROM [ProductoColores] AS [p3]

) AS [t2] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [t2].[ProductoID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p4].[ProductoMaterialID], [p4].[MaterialID], [p4].[Porcentaje], [p4].[ProductoID], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [m0].[Estado], [m0].[Nombre]
    FROM [ProductoMateriales] AS [p4]
    INNER JOIN [Materiales] AS [m0] ON [p4].[MaterialID] = [m0].[MaterialID]
) AS [t3] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [t3].[ProductoID]
LEFT JOIN [Valoraciones] AS [v] ON [p].[ProductoID] = [v].[ProductoID]
WHERE [p].[Estado] = @__p_0
ORDER BY [p].[ProductoID], [c].[CategoriaPrincipalID], [m].[MarcaID], [t].[TipoProductoID], [p0].[ProductoImagenID], [p1].[VarianteID], [t0].[ProductoTallaID], [t0].[TallaID0], [t2].[ProductoColorID], [t2].[ColorID0], [t3].[ProductoMaterialID], [t3].[MaterialID0]
